# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Task Information

## Task Title

Architectural Analysis for Multi-Tenant Configuration Auditing

## Description

PulseSphere SocialOps is a complex system monitoring platform used by multiple enterprise clients. As part of a new compliance initiative (SOC 2), a complete audit of how sensitive, user-defined configuration data is handled is required. This task focuses on tracing the lifecycle of a single piece of configuration—a user-defined alerting rule—from its creation to its execution. The system's architecture is highly decoupled, relying on event-driven patterns, and the module names are generic, requiring deep code analysis to understand their purpose.

## Your Task

Your task is to analyze the PulseSphere SocialOps codebase and produce an architectural report detailing the end-to-end data flow for a user-defined alerting rule. 

Your report must:
1.  Identify the sequence of primary modules involved in the process, starting from a hypothetical API endpoint that receives the new rule, through its validation and storage, to its use in evaluating incoming metrics, and finally to dispatching a notification.
2.  For each module in the sequence, specify its filename (e.g., `src/module_XX.ts`).
3.  For each identified module, provide a concise (1-2 sentence) description of its specific role *in this particular workflow*.
4.  Identify the core architectural pattern that decouples the components in this workflow.

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would not analyze files randomly. They would start by hypothesizing the key stages of the workflow: Configuration Ingestion, Validation, Persistence, Metric Evaluation, and Notification Dispatch.

1.  **Initial Reconnaissance:** The developer would first examine `src/config.ts` to understand the core data structures, interfaces (like `AlertRule`, `PerformanceMetric`), and potentially a shared event bus definition or constants. They would also check `package.json` for clues about dependencies or scripts.
2.  **Keyword-Driven Search:** They would then perform a codebase-wide search for keywords relevant to each stage: 
    - For ingestion: 'config', 'rule', 'create', 'update', 'api', 'http'.
    - For the main logic: 'engine', 'evaluate', 'process', 'metric', 'threshold'.
    - For communication: 'event', 'publish', 'subscribe', 'emit', 'on'.
    - For dispatch: 'notify', 'alert', 'dispatch', 'slack', 'email'.
3.  **Tracing Dependencies:** Upon identifying a candidate module (e.g., one that seems to handle rule evaluation), the developer would analyze its imports and exports to see which other modules it depends on and which modules depend on it. This helps build the connection graph.
4.  **Pattern Recognition:** By observing frequent calls to `eventBus.publish(...)` and `eventBus.subscribe(...)` (or similar patterns) across different modules, the developer would correctly identify the system's reliance on a publish-subscribe (pub/sub) or event-driven architecture.
5.  **Synthesize Findings:** Finally, they would assemble the identified modules into a logical sequence, describing how an `AlertRule` object or its associated data flows from one component to the next via events, leading to the final report.

## Evaluation Criteria

- Correctly identifies the core architectural pattern as Event-Driven or Publish/Subscribe.
- Correctly identifies at least 6 of the 8 key modules in the ground truth sequence.
- The sequence of identified modules must be logically correct, representing the flow of data.
- The description for each identified module must accurately reflect its function within this specific workflow.
- Demonstrates understanding of the separation of concerns (e.g., correctly distinguishing the Persistence Manager from the Cache).
- Correctly identifies the role of events as the communication mechanism between the decoupled modules.

30-usertool_resultRead
     1→```typescript
     2→/**************************************************************************************************
     3→ *  PulseSphere SocialOps – system_monitoring
     4→ *  File:        src/module_32.ts
     5→ *  Description: Correlates infrastructure metrics with real-time social signals.  The core engine
     6→ *               consumes two asynchronous event streams (metrics + social signals) and calculates
     7→ *               their short-term Pearson correlation inside a sliding time window.  When the
     8→ *               correlation crosses a configured threshold, a `CorrelatedAnomalyEvent` is emitted,
     9→ *               enabling downstream remediation services (auto-scaling, circuit breaking, etc.).

    11→ *  Design notes

    14→ *  • Strategy Pattern – interchangeable correlation algorithms (currently Pearson, Spearman).

116-assistanttext-
I have completed the architectural analysis for the PulseSphere SocialOps system monitoring platform. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Summary of Analysis

The PulseSphere SocialOps codebase uses an **Event-Driven Architecture** with **Publish/Subscribe** patterns as the core decoupling mechanism for the alerting rule lifecycle.

### Key Modules Identified (in sequence):

1. **`module_36.ts`** - Configuration Ingestion & Management with hot-reload capability
2. **`module_42.ts`** - Validation Pipeline using Zod schema validation
3. **`module_57.ts`** - Persistence Layer for storing correlated events
4. **`module_32.ts`** - EventBus (core pub/sub infrastructure)
5. **`module_4.ts`** - Alert Correlation Engine for metric evaluation
6. **`module_29.ts`** - Anomaly Detection & Escalation chain
7. **`module_11.ts`** - Notification Dispatch (PagerDuty, Slack, Email handlers)

### Core Architectural Patterns:

- **Event-Driven / Publish-Subscribe**: The `EventBus` class in `module_32.ts` provides `publish()` and `subscribe()` methods for topic-based communication
- **Chain-of-Responsibility**: Used for processing pipelines (Validation → Enrichment → Persistence) and escalation chains
- **Strategy Pattern**: Used for pluggable correlation and detection algorithms
- **Observer Pattern**: EventEmitter-based notifications for reactive updates

### Data Flow:

Rule Configuration → Validation → Persistence → EventBus Distribution → Metric Evaluation → Anomaly Detection → Escalation Chain → Notification Dispatch

The complete analysis has been written to `/logs/agent/solution.md` with detailed code evidence, module descriptions, and architectural diagrams.

LoggerOptions } from 'pino';\nimport { ZodError, ZodSchema } from 'zod';\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/* {\n  /**\n   * Attach an always-present correlation id to each log line.\n   * Useful when logs are piped to Loki/Grafana and queried by trace id.\n   */\n  correlationId?: string;\n}\n\n/**\n * Returns a pre-configured Pino logger instance with sensible defaults\n * for distributed tracing, timestamping and redaction of secrets.\n *\n * Each service can create child loggers per module file to keep context.\n *\n * Example:\n *   const log = createLogger({ name: 'metrics-ingestor' });\n *   const child = log.child({ component: 'kafka-consumer' });\n */\nexport function createLogger(\n  opts: CreateLoggerOptions = {},\n): Logger {\n  const {\n    correlationId,\n    level = process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',\n    ...rest\n  } = opts;\n\n  const base = {\n    pid: process.pid,\n    hostname: process.env.HOSTNAME,\n    correlationId: correlationId ?? undefined,\n  };\n\n  return pino(\n    {\n      level,\n      base,\n      timestamp: pino.stdTimeFunctions.isoTime, // 2023-05-12T08:01:55.953Z\n      redact: ['password', 'secret', '*.apiKey', '*.token'],\n      ...rest,\n    },\n    pino.destination(1), // 1 == stdout\n  );\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                  \ud83d\udecc Sleep                                  */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * Sleeps for the specified range of milliseconds.\n * Supports cancellation via AbortSignal.\n *\n * @param ms           Milliseconds to wait\n * @param abortSignal  Optional AbortSignal to cancel wait\n */\nexport function sleep(ms: number, abortSignal?: AbortSignal): Promise<void> {\n  if (ms <= 0) return Promise.resolve();\n\n  // timers/promises#setTimeout supports AbortSignal out of the box.\n  return sleepTimer(ms, undefined, { signal: abortSignal });\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                           \ud83d\udd01 Exponential Backoff                           */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nexport interface RetryOptions {\n  retries: number;            // Total retry attempts (excluding the initial try)\n  factor?: number;            // Exponential factor (default = 2)\n  minTimeout?: number;        // Initial delay in ms\n  maxTimeout?: number;        // Max cap delay in ms\n  jitter?: boolean;           // Add random jitter to each delay\n  abortSignal?: AbortSignal;  // Allows external cancellation\n  onRetry?: (\n    attempt: number,\n    error: unknown,\n    delay: number,\n  ) => void | Promise<void>;  // Hook executed before each retry sleep\n}\n\nconst DEFAULT_RETRY_OPTS: Omit<RetryOptions, 'retries'> = {\n  factor: 2,\n  minTimeout: 250,\n  maxTimeout: 15_000,\n  jitter: true,\n};\n\n/**\n * Retries an async task with (optional) exponential backoff and jitter.\n *\n * @example\n *   const json = await retryWithBackoff(() => fetchJson(url), { retries: 5 });\n */\nexport async function retryWithBackoff<T>(\n  task: () => Promise<T>,\n  {\n    retries,\n    factor,\n    minTimeout,\n    maxTimeout,\n    jitter,\n    abortSignal,\n    onRetry,\n  }: RetryOptions,\n): Promise<T> {\n  // merge defaults\n  factor = factor ?? DEFAULT_RETRY_OPTS.factor;\n  minTimeout = minTimeout ?? DEFAULT_RETRY_OPTS.minTimeout;\n  maxTimeout = maxTimeout ?? DEFAULT_RETRY_OPTS.maxTimeout;\n  jitter = jitter ?? DEFAULT_RETRY_OPTS.jitter;\n\n  let attempt = 0;\n  let lastErr: unknown;\n\n  // Use for-loop for more explicitness\n  for (; attempt <= retries; attempt++) {\n    if (abortSignal?.aborted) {\n      throw new Error('Retry aborted by AbortSignal.');\n    }\n\n    try {\n      return await task();\n    } catch (err) {\n      lastErr = err;\n\n      if (attempt === retries) break; // Exhausted\n      const exp = minTimeout! * Math.pow(factor!, attempt);\n      let delay = Math.min(exp, maxTimeout!);\n\n      // Full jitter (AWS style) => random between 0 and delay\n      if (jitter) {\n        delay = Math.random() * delay;\n      }\n\n      // eslint-disable-next-line no-await-in-loop\n      await onRetry?.(attempt + 1, err, delay);\n      // eslint-disable-next-line no-await-in-loop\n      await sleep(delay, abortSignal);\n    }\n  }\n\n  throw lastErr!;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                            \ud83e\uddf9  Safe JSON Parsing                           */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * Parse JSON without throwing for malformed input.\n *\n * Returns undefined if the input is empty or unparsable.\n * Errors are logged with a small digest and truncated input so that\n * extremely large bodies do not swamp the logs.\n */\nexport function safeJsonParse<T = any>(\n  raw: string | Buffer | null | undefined,\n  log?: Logger,\n): T | undefined {\n  if (raw == null || raw.length === 0) {\n    return undefined;\n  }\n\n  try {\n    const str = raw instanceof Buffer ? raw.toString('utf-8') : raw;\n    return JSON.parse(str) as T;\n  } catch (err) {\n    log?.warn(\n      {\n        err,\n        sample: (raw as string).toString().slice(0, 256),\n      },\n      'safeJsonParse(): Malformed JSON input.',\n    );\n    return undefined;\n  }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                           \ud83d\udcc4 Environment Loader                            */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * Loads and validates configuration from process.env (or a supplied object)\n * using a Zod schema.  Throws if validation fails so that the container\n * crashes fast and observability can alert SREs.\n *\n * @example\n *   const schema = z.object({\n *     REDIS_URL: z.string().url(),\n *     KAFKA_BROKERS: z.string(),\n *   });\n *   const cfg = loadConfig(schema); // => { REDIS_URL: 'redis://\u2026', \u2026 }\n */\nexport function loadConfig<T>(\n  schema: ZodSchema<T>,\n  env: Record<string, unknown> = process.env,\n): T {\n  const parsing = schema.safeParse(env);\n  if (!parsing.success) {\n    // Prettify zod errors & show only first 5 issues to avoid noisy logs\n    const issueSummary = parsing.error.issues\n      .slice(0, 5)\n      .map((i) => `${i.path.join('.')}: ${i.message}`)\n      .join('; expires: number }>();\n\n  constructor(private readonly defaultTtlMs = 60_000) {}\n\n  /**\n   * Get value if not expired.\n   */\n  get(key: K): V | undefined {\n    const entry = this.store.get(key);\n    if (!entry) return undefined;\n\n    if (Date.now() > entry.expires) {\n      this.store.delete(key);\n      return undefined;\n    }\n    return entry.value;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Insert or update.\n   */\n  set(key: K, value: V, ttlMs = this.defaultTtlMs): void {\n    const expires = Date.now() + ttlMs;\n    this.store.set(key, { value, expires });\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Delete entry.\n   */\n  delete(key: K): boolean {\n    return this.store.delete(key);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Remove all expired items.  Can be called periodically via setInterval.\n   */\n  sweep(): void {\n    const now = Date.now();\n    for (const [k, { expires }] of this.store) {\n      if (now > expires) this.store.delete(k);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Number of items (both expired and active).  Expired items are removed first.\n   */\n  size(): number {\n    this.sweep();\n    return this.store.size;\n  }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                     \ud83d\udd17 Correlation / Trace Id Utilities                    */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * Returns an RFC 4122 v4 UUID in base64url form which is shorter than the\n * canonical representation yet collision-safe enough for distributed tracing.\n */\nexport function generateCorrelationId(): string {\n  // Node 14.17+ supports crypto.randomUUID()\n  const uuid = crypto.randomUUID();\n\n  // Convert canonical UUID (xxxxxxxx-xxxx-xxxx-xxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx)\n  // to raw bytes, then to base64url.\n  const bytes = Buffer.from(uuid.replace(/-/g, ''), 'hex');\n  return bytes\n    .toString('base64')\n    .replace(/\\+/g, '-')\n    .replace(/\\//g, '_')\n    .replace(/=/g, '');\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                 \ud83e\uddef  Guard                                  */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * Asserts a condition at runtime, otherwise throws an error.\n * Reduces boilerplate for parameter validation.\n */\nexport function assert(\n  condition: unknown,\n  message = 'Assertion failed',\n): asserts condition {\n  if (!condition) {\n    // Include caller line for easier debugging.\n    const err = new Error(message);\n    if (Error.captureStackTrace) {\n      Error.captureStackTrace(err, assert);\n    }\n    throw err;\n  }\n}\n```",

\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport interface CorrelationEngineConfig {\n  /**\n   * Size of the sliding window (in seconds) used for correlation.\n   */\n  windowInSeconds: number;\n\n  /**\n   * Minimum amount of samples required before computing correlation.\n   */\n  minSamples: number;\n\n  /**\n   * Threshold above (absolute) which an anomaly is triggered.\n   * For Pearson, valid range is -1..1.\n   */\n  anomalyThreshold: number;\n\n  /**\n   * How often the engine will evaluate and emit correlation events (in milliseconds).\n   */\n  evaluationIntervalMs: number;\n}\n\nexport class CorrelationError extends Error {\n  constructor(message: string, public readonly cause?: unknown) {\n    super(message);\n    this.name = 'CorrelationError';\n  }\n}\n\n//#endregion\n\n//#region \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500  Sliding-Window collection  \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/**\n * Concurrent-safe, time-bounded sliding window for numeric series.\n */\nclass SlidingWindow {\n  private readonly data: Array<{ t: number; v: number }> = [];\n\n  constructor(private readonly windowMillis: number) {}\n\n  append(value: number, timestamp: number) {\n    this.data.push({ t: timestamp, v: value });\n    this.trim(timestamp);\n  }\n\n  values(): number[] {\n    return this.data.map((d) => d.v);\n  }\n\n  size(): number {\n    return this.data.length;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Removes samples that fall outside of the window.\n   */\n  private trim(currentTime: number) {\n    const threshold = currentTime - this.windowMillis;\n    // remove until first element is inside window\n    while (this.data.length > 0 && this.data[0].t < threshold) {\n      this.data.shift();\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n//#endregion\n\n//#region \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport interface CorrelationStrategy {\n  /**\n   * Computes correlation coefficient between series X and Y.\n   *\n   * Both arrays must be of equal length & >0\n   */\n  compute(x: number[], y: number[]): number;\n}\n\nexport class PearsonCorrelationStrategy implements CorrelationStrategy {\n  /* eslint-disable @typescript-eslint/no-non-null-assertion */\n  compute(x: number[], y: number[]): number {\n    if (x.length !== y.length || x.length === 0) {\n      throw new CorrelationError(\n        'Pearson requires two equally-sized, non-empty series.'\n      );\n    }\n\n    const n = x.length;\n    const sumX = x.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);\n    const sumY = y.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);\n    const sumX2 = x.reduce((a, b) => a + b * b, 0);\n    const sumY2 = y.reduce((a, b) => a + b * b, 0);\n    const sumXY = x.reduce((acc, curr, idx) => acc + curr * y[idx]!, 0);\n\n    const numerator = n * sumXY - sumX * sumY;\n    const denominator = Math.sqrt(\n      (n * sumX2 - sumX * sumX) * (n * sumY2 - sumY * sumY)\n    );\n\n    if (denominator === 0) {\n      return 0;\n    }\n\n    return numerator / denominator;\n  }\n  /* eslint-enable @typescript-eslint/no-non-null-assertion */\n}\n\n//#endregion\n\n//#region \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500 \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/**\n * Internal In production we delegate to Kafka or NATS\n * but for local dev / unit testing an EventEmitter is sufficient.\n */\nexport class EventBus extends EventEmitter {\n  publish<T>(topic: string, payload: T) {\n    this.emit(topic, payload);\n  }\n\n  subscribe<T>(\n    topic: string,\n    listener: (payload: T) => void\n  ): () => void /* unsubscribe */ {\n    this.on(topic, listener);\n    return () => this.off(topic, listener);\n  }\n}\n\n//#endregion\n\n//#region class CorrelationEngine {\n  private readonly logger = pino({ name: 'CorrelationEngine' });\n\n  private readonly metricWindow: SlidingWindow;\n  private readonly socialWindow: SlidingWindow;\n\n correlation engine, window=%ds threshold=%d',\n      this.config.windowInSeconds,\n      this.config.anomalyThreshold\n    );\n\n    this.evaluationTimer = setInterval(\n      () => this.evaluate(),\n      this.config.evaluationIntervalMs\n    );\n  }\n\n  stop(): void {\n    if (this.evaluationTimer) {\n      clearInterval(this.evaluationTimer);\n      this.evaluationTimer = undefined;\n      this.logger.info('Correlation engine stopped.');\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Observer callback for infrastructure metrics.\n   */\n  onMetric(metric: InfraMetric) {\n    try {\n      if (!Number.isFinite(metric.value)) return;\n\n      this.metricWindow.append(metric.value, metric.timestamp);\n      this.metricName ??= metric.metricName; // set first time\n      this.logger.debug({ metric }, 'Metric appended to window.');\n    } catch (err) {\n      this.logger.error({ err, metric }, 'Failed to process metric.');\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Observer callback for social signals.\n   */\n  onSocialSignal(signal: SocialSignal) {\n    try {\n      if (!Number.isFinite(signal.value)) return;\n\n      this.socialWindow.append(signal.value, signal.timestamp);\n      this.signalType this.logger.debug(\n          'Not enough samples (%d/%d) \u2013 skipping evaluation.',\n          Math.min(this.metricWindow.size(), this.socialWindow.size()),\n          this.config.minSamples\n Implements the Strategy pattern so that\n *               SRE teams can hot-swap correlation algorithms at runtime (via dynamic\n *               configuration pushed through the platform\u2019s configuration-management\n *               microservice).\n *\n *  Key Patterns:\n *      \u2022 Strategy Pattern      \u2013 Pluggable correlation algorithms\n *      \u2022 Observer (RxJS)       \u2013 Stream/buffer telemetry events\n *      \u2022 Command Pattern       \u2013 Publishes alert commands to message bus\n *      \u2022 Error-handling        \u2013 Fault-tolerant, production-grade\n *\n *  Author:      PulseSphere Core Engineering\n ****************************************************************************************/\n\nimport { Subject, Observable, bufferTime, filter, map } from 'rxjs';\nimport { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid';\nimport dayjs from 'dayjs';\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                                Domain Types                                */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/** Social context that accompanies every telemetry datapoint */\nexport interface SocialContext {\n  likes: number;\n  comments: number;\n  shares: number;\n  liveStreamViewers: number;\n  trendingHashtags?: string[];\n}\n\n/** Raw telemetry emitted by lower-level collectors */\nexport interface TelemetryEvent {\n  readonly id: string;               // Unique identifier for the metric datapoint\n  readonly metric: string;           // e.g. cpu.utilization, api.latency\n  readonly value: number;\n  readonly timestamp: number;        // epoch-ms\n  readonly tags?: Record<string, string>;\n  readonly social: SocialContext;    // Social dimension\n}\n\n/** Correlated alert dispatched to downstream Alerting-MS */\nexport interface Alert {\n  readonly id: string;\n  readonly severity: 'INFO' | 'WARN' | 'CRITICAL';\n  readonly title: string;\n  readonly description: string;\n  readonly createdAt: number;\n  readonly correlatedEvents: string[]; // list of TelemetryEvent.id\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                     Infrastructure / Adapter Layer (Ports)                 */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * Simplified interface for the platform\u2019s configuration service.\n * It supports live-reloading and notifies subscribers on updates.\n */\nexport interface ConfigurationService {\n  get<T = unknown>(path: string): T;\n  onChange(path: string): Observable<unknown>;\n}\n\n/**\n * Outbound port for the event bus. In production this will be implemented\n * via NATS or Apache Kafka; we only need the contract for compilation.\n */\nexport interface MessageBus {\n  publish<T>(topic: string, message: T, headers?: Record<string, string>): Promise<void>;\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                       Correlation Strategy \u2013 Abstraction                   */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * Strategy pattern for correlation. Each implementation analyses the buffered\n * telemetry events and decides if/when an Alert must be raised.\n */\nexport interface AlertCorrelationStrategy {\n  /**\n   * Analyses a batch (time-window) of telemetry events and emits zero or more Alerts.\n   * @param events  \u2013 All telemetry events gathered within the window\n   */\n  correlate(events: ReadonlyArray<TelemetryEvent>): Alert[];\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*           Concrete Strategies \u2013 Used by AlertCorrelationEngine             */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * Simple threshold-based strategy. Demonstrates how social amplification\n * (likes/shares) can raise severity.\n */\nexport class ThresholdStrategy implements AlertCorrelationStrategy {\n  private readonly cpuThreshold: number;\n  private readonly socialAmplificationFactor: number;\n\n  constructor(options: { cpuThreshold: number; amplificationFactor: number }) {\n    this.cpuThreshold = options.cpuThreshold;\n    this.socialAmplificationFactor = options.amplificationFactor;\n  }\n\n  correlate(events: ReadonlyArray<TelemetryEvent>): Alert[] {\n    const alerts: Alert[] = [];\n\n    events\n      .filter((e) => e.metric === 'cpu.utilization')\n      .forEach((event) => {\n        const amplification =\n          1 +\n          (event.social.likes + event.social.comments + event.social.shares) /\n            10_000; // amplify threshold by social heat\n\n        if (event.value >= this.cpuThreshold / amplification) {\n          alerts.push({\n            id: uuidv4(),\n            severity: amplification > this.socialAmplificationFactor ? 'CRITICAL' : 'WARN',\n            title: 'High CPU detected',\n            description: `CPU utilization ${event.value.toFixed(\n              2\n            )}% surpassed threshold (${this.cpuThreshold}%). Social amplification=${\n              amplification.toFixed(2)\n            }.`,\n            createdAt: Date.now(),\n            correlatedEvents: [event.id],\n          });\n        }\n      });\n\n    return alerts;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Trending-hashtag strategy. If an influencer surge is detected together with rising\n * latency metrics, promote the alert to CRITICAL.\n */\nexport class TrendingHashtagStrategy implements AlertCorrelationStrategy {\n  private readonly latencyP99ThresholdMs: number;\n  private readonly hashtagSurgeThreshold: number;\n\n  constructor(opts: { latencyP99ThresholdMs: number; hashtagSurgeThreshold: number }) {\n    this.latencyP99ThresholdMs = opts.latencyP99ThresholdMs;\n    this.hashtagSurgeThreshold = opts.hashtagSurgeThreshold;\n  }\n\n  correlate(events: ReadonlyArray<TelemetryEvent>): Alert[] {\n    const alerts: Alert[] = [];\n\n    const latencyEvents = events.filter((e) => e.metric === 'api.latency.p99');\n    const trendingEvents = events.filter(\n      (e) => e.social.trendingHashtags && e.social.trendingHashtags.length > 0\n    );\n\n    // If both latency high AND trending hashtags surging, create incident.\n    const hasLatencyIssue = latencyEvents.some((e) => e.value >= this.latencyP99ThresholdMs);\n    const trendingScore =\n      trendingEvents.reduce(\n        (acc, ev) => acc + (ev.social.trendingHashtags?.length ?? 0),\n        0\n      ) / Math.max(trendingEvents.length, 1);\n\n    if (hasLatencyIssue && trendingScore >= this.hashtagSurgeThreshold) {\n      const correlatedIds = [...latencyEvents, ...trendingEvents].map((e) => e.id);\n\n      alerts.push({\n        id: uuidv4(),\n        severity: 'CRITICAL',\n        title: 'Latency spike during trending hashtag surge',\n        description: `P99 latency exceeded ${\n          this.latencyP99ThresholdMs\n        }ms while trending activity score=${trendingScore.toFixed(\n          2\n        )}. Potential virality overload.`,\n        createdAt: Date.now(),\n        correlatedEvents: correlatedIds,\n      });\n    }\n\n    return alerts;\n  }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                      Strategy Factory (Runtime Switch)                     */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\ntype StrategyDescriptor =\n  | { kind: 'threshold'; params: { cpuThreshold: number; amplificationFactor: number } }\n  | { kind: 'trending'; params: { latencyP99ThresholdMs: number; hashtagSurgeThreshold: number } };\n\n/**\n * Simplistic factory that instantiates correlation strategies based on config.\n * This allows runtime re-configuration without downtime.\n */\nexport class StrategyFactory {\n  public static create(descriptor: StrategyDescriptor): AlertCorrelationStrategy {\n    switch (descriptor.kind) {\n      case 'threshold':\n        return new ThresholdStrategy(descriptor.params);\n\n      case 'trending':\n        return new TrendingHashtagStrategy(descriptor.params);\n\n      default:\n        // TypeScript exhaustive check\n        // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/restrict-template-expressions\n        throw new Error(`Unsupported strategy: ${(descriptor as any).kind}`);\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                        Alert Correlation Engine (Core)                     */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\ninterface EngineOptions {\n  bufferInMs: number; // Size of window for buffering telemetry events\n  telemetryStream$: Observable<TelemetryEvent>;\n  configService: ConfigurationService;\n  bus: MessageBus;\n  logger?: (msg: string, meta?: unknown) => void;\n}\n\n/**\n * Main engine responsible for:\n *   1. Buffering/aggregating telemetry events.\n *   2. Delegating to current correlation strategy.\n *   3. Publishing resulting alerts to the message bus.\n *   4. Reacting to dynamic configuration changes.\n */\nexport class AlertCorrelationEngine {\n  private readonly telemetry$ = new Subject<TelemetryEvent>();\n  private currentStrategy: AlertCorrelationStrategy;\n  private readonly strategyConfigPath = 'alerting.correlation.strategy';\n  private readonly logger: (msg: string, meta?: unknown) => void;\n\n  constructor(private readonly options: EngineOptions) {\n    this.logger = options.logger ?? console.log;\n\n    // Bootstrap initial strategy\n    const initialDescriptor = options.configService.get<StrategyDescriptor>(\n      this.strategyConfigPath\n    );\n    this.currentStrategy = StrategyFactory.create(initialDescriptor);\n\n    // Subscribe to config changes to hot-swap strategies\n    options.configService\n      .onChange(this.strategyConfigPath)\n      .subscribe((newDescriptor) => this.updateStrategy(newDescriptor as StrategyDescriptor));\n\n    // Wire telemetry stream\n    options.telemetryStream$.subscribe({\n      next: (ev) => this.telemetry$.next(ev),\n      error: (err) => this.logger('Telemetry stream failure', err),\n    });\n\n    // Start pipeline\n    this.initProcessingPipeline();\n  }\n\n  /** Hot-swaps the active strategy safely. */\n  private updateStrategy(descriptor: StrategyDescriptor): void {\n    try {\n      this.logger(`Switching correlation strategy \u2192 ${descriptor.kind}`);\n      this.currentStrategy = StrategyFactory.create(descriptor);\n    } catch (err) {\n      this.logger('Strategy swap failed, keeping previous strategy', err);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /** Builds the RxJS pipeline in charge of buffering + correlation + publication. */\n  private initProcessingPipeline(): void {\n    this.telemetry$\n      .pipe(\n        bufferTime(this.options.bufferInMs), // create tumbling window\n        filter((batch) => batch.length > 0),\n        map((batch) => this.safeCorrelate(batch)) // catch errors inside correlation\n      )\n      .subscribe({\n        next: (alerts) => alerts.forEach((a) => this.publishAlert(a)),\n        error: (err) => this.logger('Correlation pipeline failure', err),\n      });\n  }\n\n  /** Wraps strategy.correlate() with error handling so that one bad batch doesn\u2019t kill the stream. */\n  private safeCorrelate(batch: TelemetryEvent[]): Alert[] {\n    try {\n      return this.currentStrategy.correlate(batch);\n    } catch (err) {\n      this.logger('Correlation error', err);\n      return [];\n    }\n  }\n\n  private async publishAlert(alert: Alert): Promise<void> {\n    try {\n      await this.options.bus.publish<Alert>('alerts', alert, {\n        'x-correlation-id': alert.id,\n        'x-generated-at': dayjs(alert.createdAt).toISOString(),\n      });\n      this.logger(`Alert published (${alert.severity})`, alert);\n    } catch (err) {\n      // We can add retry/backoff logic here\n      this.logger('Failed to publish alert', { alert, error: err });\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                 Example Bootstrap (would live elsewhere in prod)           */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * This bootstrap is for demonstration/testing only. Real deployments will\n * wire the engine inside an application server/container with DI.\n */\nif (require.main === module) {\n  /* eslint-disable @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any */\n  const mockConfigService: ConfigurationService = {\n    get: <T>(path: string): T =>\n      ({\n        kind: 'threshold',\n        params: { cpuThreshold: 80, amplificationFactor: 1.3 },\n      } as unknown as T),\n\n    onChange: (_path: string): Observable<unknown> => new Subject<unknown>(),\n  };\n\n  const mockBus: MessageBus = {\n    publish: async <T>(_topic: string, _message: T): Promise<void> => {\n      /* noop */\n    },\n  };\n\n  // Simulate telemetry stream\n  const telemetry$ = new Subject<TelemetryEvent>();\n  const engine = new AlertCorrelationEngine({\n    bufferInMs: 5_000,\n    telemetryStream$: telemetry$,\n    configService: mockConfigService,\n    bus: mockBus,\n  });\n\n  // Emit demo telemetry every second\n  setInterval(() => {\n    telemetry$.next({\n      id: uuidv4(),\n      metric: 'cpu.utilization',\n      value: Math.random() * 100,\n      timestamp: Date.now(),\n      social: {\n        likes: Math.floor(Math.random() * 3_000),\n        comments: Math.floor(Math.random() * 500),\n        shares: Math.floor(Math.random() * 200),\n        liveStreamViewers: Math.floor(Math.random() * 10_000),\n      },\n    });\n  }, 1_000);\n\n  // Simulate latency + hashtag spike\n  setInterval(() => {\n    telemetry$.next({\n      id: uuidv4(),\n      metric: 'api.latency.p99',\n      value: 600 + Math.random() * 400,\n      timestamp: Date.now(),\n      social: {\n        likes: 0,\n        comments: 0,\n        shares: 0,\n        liveStreamViewers: 0,\n        trendingHashtags: ['#PulzeSphereRocks', '#Viral'],\n      },\n    });\n  }, 7_000);\n\n  // eslint-disable-next-line no-console\n  console.log('Demo AlertCorrelationEngine started. * Encapsulates a backup request so that it can be queued, retried or persisted.\n */\nexport class BackupCommand {\n    constructor(public readonly strategy: BackupStrategy) {}\n\n    execute(): Promise<BackupResult> {\n        return this.strategy.execute();\n    }\n}\n\nclass BackupExecutor {\n    private running = 0;\n    private readonly queue: BackupCommand[] = [];\n    private readonly logger: Logger;\n\n    constructor(\n        private readonly cfgService: ConfigurationService,\n        rootLogger: Logger,\n    ) {\n        this.logger = rootLogger.child({ module: 'BackupExecutor' });\n    }\n\n    async dispatch(cmd: BackupCommand): Promise<BackupResult> {\n        if (this.running >= this.cfgService.current.maxConcurrentBackups) {\n            this.logger.warn(\n                'Maximum concurrent backups reached. Queuing command...',\n            );\n            return new Promise<BackupResult>((resolve) => {\n                this.queue.push(\n                    new BackupCommandProxy(cmd, resolve, this.logger),\n                );\n            });\n        }\n        return this.runCommand(cmd);\n    }\n\n    private async runCommand(cmd: BackupCommand): Promise<BackupResult> {\n        this.running++;\n        try {\n            const result = await cmd.execute();\n            return result;\n        } finally {\n            this.running--;\n            // Drain queue if possible\n            if (this.queue.length > 0) {\n                const next = this.queue.shift()!;\n                // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-floating-promises\n                this.runCommand(next.original).then(next.resolve);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Proxy holding callback to resolve a deferred backup result.\n */\nclass BackupCommandProxy {\n   }\n\n    async handle(ctx: RecoveryContext): Promise<void> {\n        if (this.next) {\n            await this.next.handle(ctx);\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nclass DownloadSnapshotHandler extends 20 || trendingScore > 90) {\n    return AlertSeverity.CRITICAL;\n  }\n  if (cpu > 80 || errorRate > 15 || trendingScore > 80) {\n    return AlertSeverity.HIGH;\n  }\n  if (cpu > 70 || errorRate > 10 || trendingScore > 70) {\n    return AlertSeverity.MEDIUM;\n  }\n  return AlertSeverity.LOW;\n}\n\n/**\n * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n */\n\nclass MetricConsumer {\n  private readonly kafka: Kafka;\n  private readonly consumer: });\n\n    this.started = true;\n    logger.info('Metric consumer started');\n  }\n\n  async stop(): Promise<void> {\n    if (!this.started) return;\n    await this.consumer.disconnect();\n Replace stubs with concrete implementations in\n *    production (e.g. Prometheus queries, PagerDuty SDK calls\u2026).\n *  \u2022 Configuration is expected via environment variables; see README.\n */\n\nimport { EventEmitter } from 'events';\nimport { Kafka, logLevel, Consumer, EachMessagePayload } from 'kafkajs';\nimport pino from 'pino';\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/*                         Logger (shared utility)                    */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\nconst logger = pino({\n  name: 'module_29:anomaly-detector',\n  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL ?? 'info',\n});\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/*                                Types                               */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\n/**\n * Raw, enriched telemetry event.\n */\nexport interface MetricEvent {\n  service: string; // e.g. \"timeline-api\"\n  host: string; // e.g. \"ip-10-2-3-4\"\n  timestamp: number; // epoch millis\n  metrics: {\n    cpuUtilization: number; // 0\u20131\n    memoryUtilization: number; // 0\u20131\n    p95LatencyMs: number;\n    requestRateRps: number;\n  };\n  socialSignals: {\n    likes: number;\n    comments: number;\n    shares: number;\n    liveStreamViewers: number;\n  };\n  tags?: Record<string, string>;\n}\n\n/**\n * Anomaly detection result.\n */\nexport interface DetectionResult {\n  isAnomaly: boolean;\n  severity: Severity;\n  reason: string;\n  strategy: string;\n}\n\nexport enum Severity {\n  Low = 'low',\n  Medium = 'medium',\n  High = 'high',\n  Critical = 'critical',\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/*                         Strategy Pattern                           */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\n/**\n * Pluggable detection strategy contract.\n */\nexport interface DetectionStrategy {\n  readonly name: string;\n  detect(event: MetricEvent): DetectionResult | null;\n}\n\n/**\n * CPU Spike strategy \u2013 identifies sudden CPU utilisation > 85%.\n */\nexport class CpuSpikeStrategy implements DetectionStrategy {\n  readonly name = 'cpu_spike';\n\n  detect(event: MetricEvent): DetectionResult | null {\n    const { cpuUtilization } = event.metrics;\n    if (cpuUtilization > 0.85) {\n      return {\n        isAnomaly: true,\n        severity: cpuUtilization > 0.95 ? Severity.Critical : Severity.High,\n        reason: `CPU utilisation at ${(cpuUtilization * 100).toFixed(2)}%`,\n        strategy: this.name,\n      };\n    }\n    return null;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Memory Leak strategy \u2013 memory > 90%.\n */\nexport class MemoryLeakStrategy implements DetectionStrategy {\n  readonly name = 'memory_leak';\n\n  detect(event: MetricEvent): DetectionResult | null {\n    const { memoryUtilization } = event.metrics;\n    if (memoryUtilization > 0.9) {\n      return {\n        isAnomaly: true,\n        severity:\n          memoryUtilization > 0.97 ? Severity.Critical : Severity.High,\n        reason: `Memory utilisation at ${(memoryUtilization * 100).toFixed(\n          2,\n        )}%`,\n        strategy: this.name,\n      };\n    }\n    return null;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Viral Surge strategy \u2013 sudden user interest (shares + likes) combined\n * with rising latency.\n */\nexport class ViralSurgeStrategy implements DetectionStrategy {\n  readonly name = 'viral_surge';\n\n  private readonly SOCIAL_THRESHOLD = 10_000; // customizable\n\n  detect(event: MetricEvent): DetectionResult | null {\n    const socialScore =\n      event.socialSignals.likes +\n      event.socialSignals.comments +\n      event.socialSignals.shares +\n      event.socialSignals.liveStreamViewers;\n\n    if (\n      socialScore > this.SOCIAL_THRESHOLD &&\n      event.metrics.p95LatencyMs > 250\n    ) {\n      return {\n        isAnomaly: true,\n        severity:\n          socialScore > this.SOCIAL_THRESHOLD * 2\n            ? Severity.Critical\n            : Severity.Medium,\n        reason: `Viral surge detected (${socialScore} interactions) with latency ${\n          event.metrics.p95LatencyMs\n        } ms`,\n        strategy: this.name,\n      };\n    }\n    return null;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Strategy registry allowing dynamic plug-in/out at runtime.\n */\nexport class StrategyRegistry {\n  private readonly strategies = new Map<string, DetectionStrategy>();\n\n  register(strategy: DetectionStrategy) {\n    if (this.strategies.has(strategy.name)) {\n      logger.warn({ strategy: strategy.name }, 'Strategy already registered');\n      return;\n    }\n    this.strategies.set(strategy.name, strategy);\n    logger.info({ strategy: strategy.name }, 'Strategy registered');\n  }\n\n  unregister(name: string) {\n    this.strategies.delete(name);\n    logger.info({ name }, 'Strategy unregistered');\n  }\n\n  detect(event: MetricEvent): DetectionResult[] {\n    const results: DetectionResult[] = [];\n    for (const strategy of this.strategies.values()) {\n      try {\n        const result = strategy.detect(event);\n        if (result?.isAnomaly) results.push(result);\n      } catch (err) {\n        logger.error(\n          { err, strategy: strategy.name },\n          'Strategy execution error',\n        );\n      }\n    }\n    return results;\n  }\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/*                          Observer Pattern                          */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\nexport interface AnomalyEvent {\n  metric: MetricEvent;\n  detections: DetectionResult[];\n}\n\nexport type AnomalyListener = (anomaly: AnomalyEvent) => void;\n\n/**\n * Emits \"anomaly\" events to registered listeners.\n */\nexport class AnomalyDetector extends EventEmitter {\n  private readonly registry: StrategyRegistry;\n\n  constructor(registry: StrategyRegistry) {\n    super();\n    this.registry = registry;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Evaluate a single metric event.\n   */\n  evaluate(event: MetricEvent): void {\n    const detections = this.registry.detect(event);\n    if (detections.length) {\n      const anomaly: AnomalyEvent = { metric: event, detections };\n      this.emit('anomaly', anomaly);\n    }\n  }\n\n  addListener(listener: AnomalyListener): void {\n    super.addListener('anomaly', listener);\n  }\n\n  removeListener(listener: AnomalyListener): void {\n    super.removeListener('anomaly', listener);\n  }\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/*                  Chain-of-Responsibility: Escalation               */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\nexport interface EscalationContext {\n  anomaly: AnomalyEvent;\n}\n\nexport abstract class EscalationHandler {\n  private next?: EscalationHandler;\n\n  setNext(next: EscalationHandler): EscalationHandler {\n    this.next = next;\n    return next;\n  }\n\n  async handle(ctx: EscalationContext): Promise<void> {\n    const handled = await this.process(ctx).catch((err) => {\n      logger.error({ err }, 'Handler process failed');\n      return false;\n    });\n\n    if (!handled && this.next) {\n      await this.next.handle(ctx);\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Return true if the handler fully handled the anomaly (no further\n   * escalation needed).\n   */\n  protected abstract process(ctx: EscalationContext): Promise<boolean>;\n}\n\n/**\n * AutoScaler handler \u2013 tries to resolve by adding capacity.\n */\nexport class AutoScalerHandler extends EscalationHandler {\n  protected async process(ctx: EscalationContext): Promise<boolean> {\n    const { anomaly } = ctx;\n    const maxSeverity = getMaxSeverity(anomaly.detections);\n\n    if (maxSeverity === Severity.Low || maxSeverity === Severity.Medium) {\n      const service = anomaly.metric.service;\n      logger.info(\n        { service },\n        'Triggering auto-scaler (kubernetes/hpa) for service',\n      );\n      // TODO: Replace with real orchestrator API call.\n      await fakeNetworkDelay();\n      // Assume scaling succeeded.\n      return true;\n    }\n    return false; // escalate further\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Alert handler \u2013 sends PagerDuty / Slack alerts.\n */\nexport class AlertHandler extends EscalationHandler {\n  protected async process(ctx: EscalationContext): Promise<boolean> {\n    const { anomaly } = ctx;\n    const maxSeverity = getMaxSeverity(anomaly.detections);\n\n    logger.info(\n      { maxSeverity, service: anomaly.metric.service },\n      'Sending alert',\n    );\n    try {\n      // TODO: Integrate with PagerDuty SDK.\n      await fakeNetworkDelay();\n      return maxSeverity !== Severity.Critical; // escalate if critical\n    } catch (err) {\n      logger.error({ err }, 'Alert dispatch failed');\n      return false;\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Final escalation \u2013 page incident commander.\n */\nexport class IncidentCommanderHandler extends EscalationHandler {\n  protected async process(ctx: EscalationContext): Promise<boolean> {\n    const { anomaly } = ctx;\n    logger.warn(\n      { anomaly },\n      'Escalating to Incident Commander \u2013 human intervention required',\n    );\n    // Fail-safe: always considered handled after this.\n    await fakeNetworkDelay();\n    return true;\n  }\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/*                     Kafka Consumer Integration                     */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\nexport class AnomalyDetectionService {\n  private readonly detector: AnomalyDetector;\n  private readonly kafka: Kafka;\n  private consumer?: Consumer;\n  private readonly escalationChain: EscalationHandler;\n\n  constructor() {\n    // Strategies\n    const registry = new StrategyRegistry();\n    registry.register(new CpuSpikeStrategy());\n    registry.register(new MemoryLeakStrategy());\n    registry.register(new ViralSurgeStrategy());\n\n    // Detector\n    this.detector = new AnomalyDetector(registry);\n\n    // Escalation chain\n    const autoScaler = new AutoScalerHandler();\n    const alertHandler = new AlertHandler();\n    const commander = new IncidentCommanderHandler();\n    autoScaler.setNext(alertHandler).setNext(commander);\n    this.escalationChain = autoScaler;\n\n    // Observers\n    this.detector.addListener((anomaly) => {\n      this.escalationChain\n        .handle({ anomaly })\n        .catch((err) =>\n          logger.error({ err }, 'Unhandled error during escalation'),\n        );\n    });\n\n    // Kafka\n    this.kafka = new Kafka({\n      clientId: 'pulse-sphere-anomaly-detector',\n      brokers: (process.env.KAFKA_BROKERS ?? 'localhost:9092').split(','),\n      logLevel: logLevel.ERROR,\n    });\n  }\n\n  async start(): Promise<void> {\n    const topic = process.env.TELEMETRY_TOPIC ?? 'telemetry.enriched';\n    const groupId =\n      process.env.CONSUMER_GROUP_ID ?? 'anomaly-detector-consumer';\n\n    this.consumer = this.kafka.consumer({ groupId });\n    await this.consumer.connect();\n    await this.consumer.subscribe({ topic, fromBeginning: false });\n\n    logger.info({ topic, groupId }, 'Kafka consumer connected');\n\n    await this.consumer.run({\n      eachMessage: async (payload: EachMessagePayload) => {\n        try {\n          const event = JSON.parse(\n            payload.message.value!.toString('utf8'),\n          ) as MetricEvent;\n          this.detector.evaluate(event);\n        } catch (err) {\n          logger.warn({ err }, 'Invalid metric event received');\n        }\n      },\n    });\n  }\n\n  async stop(): Promise<void> {\n    if (this.consumer) {\n      await this.consumer.disconnect();\n      logger.info('Kafka consumer disconnected');\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/*                            Utilities                               */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\nfunction getMaxSeverity(detections: DetectionResult[]): Severity {\n  const ranking: Severity[] = [\n    Severity.Low,\n    Severity.Medium,\n    Severity.High,\n    Severity.Critical,\n  ];\n  return detections.reduce<Severity>(\n    (prev, curr) =>\n      ranking.indexOf(curr.severity) > ranking.indexOf(prev)\n        ? curr.severity\n        : prev,\n    Severity.Low,\n  );\n}\n\n/**\n * Simulates network I/O latency for stubbed external calls.\n */\nasync function fakeNetworkDelay(): Promise<void> {\n  return new Promise((res) =>\n    setTimeout(res, Math.random() * 200 + 100 /* 100\u2013300ms */),\n  );\n}\n\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n/*                       Module singleton export                      */\n/* ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\nexport const anomalyDetectionService = new AnomalyDetectionService();\n\n/**\n * Auto-start when executed directly (useful for Docker entrypoints):\n *\n *   node dist/module_29.js\n */\nif (require.main === module) {\n  anomalyDetectionService\n    .start()\n    .then(() => {\n      logger.info('Anomaly detection service started');\n    })\n    .catch((err) => {\n      logger.fatal({ err }, 'Failed to start anomaly detection service');\n      process.exit(1);\n    });\n\n  // Graceful shutdown\n  process.on('SIGINT', async () => {\n    logger.info('Stopping anomaly detection service\u2026');\n    await anomalyDetectionService.stop();\n    process.exit(0);\n  });\n}\n```",

constructor(\n    private readonly meshClient: ServiceMeshClient,\n    private readonly highWaterMarkPct = 75,\n    private readonly lowWaterMarkPct  = 35,\n  ) {}\n\n  evaluate(metric: metric.trendingScore >= 0.95;\n    if (isCrit) {\n      await AlertChannel.pagerDuty(\n        `\ud83d\udea8 CRITICAL: ${metric.appId} likely overloaded! ` +\n        `cpu=${metric.cpuPct}% */\n/*                              Service-mesh client                           */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nclass ServiceMeshClient {\n  private readonly http: AxiosInstance;\n\n  constructor(\n    readonly baseURL: string = process.env.SERVICE_MESH_BASE_URL ?? 'http://mesh-gateway',\n    readonly timeout = 5_000,\n  ) {\n    this.http = axios.create({ baseURL: this.baseURL, timeout: this.timeout });\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Scale an application up/down by \"factor\" replicas.\n   * This interacts with the platform orchestrator through\n   * the mesh sidecar.\n   */\n  public async scale(appId: string, factor: number): Promise<void> {\n    try {\n      await this.http.post(`/apps/${appId}/scale`, { factor });\n      console.info(`[Scale] ${appId} scaled by ${factor}`);\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error(`[Scale] Failed to scale ${appId}:`, err);\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                              Alerting helpers                              */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nclass AlertChannel {\n  static async slack(message: string): Promise<void> {\n    // Placeholder: in production we'd push to Slack webhook\n    console.log(`[Slack] ${message}`);\n  }\n\n  static async pagerDuty(message: string): Promise<void> {\n    // Placeholder: integration key & routing will sit in vault\n    console.log(`[PagerDuty] ${message}`);\n  }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                            Main Orchestrator Class                         */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nexport class SocialAwareAutoScaler {\n  private readonly kafka: Kafka;\n  private readonly meshClient = new ServiceMeshClient();\n  private readonly eventBus = new MetricEventBus();\n  private readonly strategies: ScalingStrategy[] = [];\n  private readonly alertChain: AlertHandler;\n  private isShuttingDown = false;\n\n  constructor(\n    private readonly kafkaBrokers: string[] = (process.env.KAFKA_BROKERS ?? // one strategy acted \u2013 avoid conflicting actions\n        } catch (err) {\n          console.error('[AutoScaler] Command failed:', err);\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Converts Kafka payload into EnrichedMetric object with validation.\n   */\n  private parseMetric({ message }: EachMessagePayload): EnrichedMetric | undefined {\n    try {\n      if (!message.value) return;\n      const obj = JSON.parse(message.value.toString());\n\n      /* Lightweight validation */\n      const metric: EnrichedMetric = {\n        appId          : obj.appId,\n        cpuPct         : Number(obj.cpuPct),\n        memPct         : Number(obj.memPct),\n        sentimentScore : Number(obj.sentimentScore),\n        trendingScore  : Number(obj.trendingScore),\n        timestamp      : Number(obj.timestamp),\n      };\n\n      if (!metric.appId || Number.isNaN(metric.cpuPct)) {\n        throw new Error('Invalid metric shape');\n      }\n      return metric;\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.warn('[AutoScaler] Discarded malformed metric:', err);\n      return;\n    }\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Shutdown hook \u2013 ensures consumer disconnect & drains inflight tasks.\n   */\n  private async shutdown(): Promise<void> {\n    if (this.isShuttingDown) return;\n    this.isShuttingDown = true;\n\n    console.info('[AutoScaler] Shutting down\u2026');\n    // Additional cleanup (HTTP, etc.) could be awaited here.\n  }\n}\n\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*                     Module bootstrap (only when run directly)              */\n/* -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\nif (require.main === module) {\n  (async () => {\n    try {\n      const scaler = new SocialAwareAutoScaler();\n      await scaler.start();\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('[AutoScaler] Fatal:', err);\n      process.exitCode = 1;\n    }\n  })();\n}\n```",

         // epoch millis\n    readonly signalType: 'like' | 'comment' | 'share' | 'livestream_view';\n    readonly magnitude: number;          // absolute delta observed\n    readonly region?: string;              // correlation score in range [0, 1]\n    readonly riskLevel: 'LOW' | 'MEDIUM' | 'HIGH' | 'CRITICAL';\n}\n\n/* ============================================================================\n *  Observer Pattern\n * ========================================================================== */\n\nexport interface CorrelatedEventObserver {\n    onCorrelatedEvent(event: CorrelatedEvent): void | Promise<void>;\n}\n\n/* ============================================================================\n *  Correlation Strategy Pattern\n * ========================================================================== */\n\nexport interface CorrelationStrategy {\n    /**\n     * Computes a correlation score between a metric and a social signal.\n     * Return in the inclusive range [0, 1].\n     *\n     * Returning NaN signals \u201cunable to correlate\u201d.\n     */\n    compute(\n        metric: SystemMetricEvent,\n        signal: SocialSignalEvent | null\n    ): number;\n}\n\n/**\n * Default implementation that gives higher weight to memory/cpu spikes during high\n * magnitude social events.\n */\nexport class WeightedCorrelationStrategy implements CorrelationStrategy {\n    compute(\n        metric: SystemMetricEvent,\n        signal: SocialSignalEvent | null\n    ): number {\n        if (!signal) return 0;\n\n        const metricFactor =\n            metric.metric.startsWith('cpu') || metric.metric.startsWith('memory')\n                ? 0.6\n                : 0.4;\n\n        // Normalise values: naive min-max assumption for demo purposes.\n        const normalisedMetric = Math.min(metric.value / 100, 1); // e.g. 90% CPU = 0.9\n        const normalisedSocial = Math.min(signal.magnitude / 10_000, 1);\n\n        const score = metricFactor * normalisedMetric + (1 - metricFactor) * normalisedSocial;\n\n        return Number.isNaN(score) ? 0 : Math.min(score, 1);\n    }\n}\n\n/* ============================================================================\n *  Chain-of-Responsibility for CorrelatedEvent processing\n * ========================================================================== */\n\ninterface PipelineStep {\n    handle(event: CorrelatedEvent, next: () => Promise<void>): Promise<void>;\n}\n\nclass ValidationStep implements PipelineStep {\n    private readonly ajv = new Ajv({ allErrors: true, removeAdditional: true });\n    private readonly validator: ValidateFunction<CorrelatedEvent>;\n\n    constructor() {\n        const schema = {\n            type: 'object',\n            required: [\n                'timestamp',\n                'metricHost',\n                'metricName',\n                'metricValue',\n                'score',\n                'riskLevel'\n            ]\n            // Additional JSON schema details intentionally omitted for brevity\n        };\n        this.validator = this.ajv.compile(schema);\n    }\n\n    async handle(event: CorrelatedEvent, next: () => Promise<void>): Promise<void> {\n        if (!this.validator(event)) {\n            throw new Error(\n                `CorrelatedEvent validation failed: ${this.ajv.errorsText(this.validator.errors)}`\n            );\n        }\n        await next();\n    }\n}\n\nclass EnrichmentStep implements PipelineStep {\n    async handle(event: CorrelatedEvent, next: () => Promise<void>): Promise<void> {\n        // Enrich riskLevel based on score.\n        const risk =\n            event.score >= 0.85\n                ? 'MEDIUM'\n                : 'LOW';\n\n        (event as any).riskLevel = risk; // Type cast for mutation inside pipeline.\n        await next();\n    }\n}\n\nclass PersistenceStep implements PipelineStep {\n    constructor(private readonly logger: winston.Logger) {}\n\n    async handle(event: CorrelatedEvent, next: () => Promise<void>): Promise<void> {\n        // In production we\u2019d winston.createLogger({\n                level: 'info',\n                transports: [new winston.transports.Console()]\n            });\n\n        this.kafka = new Kafka({\n            clientId: registerObserver(observer: CorrelatedEventObserver): () => void {\n        this.observers.add(observer);\n        return () => this.observers.delete(observer);\n    }\n\n    /*                     this.metricStream$.next(event);\n                    } catch (err) {\n                        this.logger.error('Failed to deserialize metric event', { err });\n this.socialStream$.next(event);\n                    } catch (err) {\n                        this.logger.error('Failed to deserialize social event', { err });\n                    }\n                }\n            });\n        };\n\n        connectAndSubscribe().catch(err =>\n            this.logger.error('Kafka subscription failure', { err })\n        );\n    }\n\n    /* private wireCorrelationStream(): void {\n        const bufferWindow = this.config.bufferWindowMs ?? 5_000;\n\n        // Merge both streams into correlated events every `bufferWindow`.\n        const correlated$: Observable<CorrelatedEvent> = merge(\n            this.metricStream$.pipe(map(e => ({ type: 'metric' as const, event: e }))),\n            this.socialStream$.pipe(map(e => ({ type: 'social' as const, event: e })))\n        ).pipe(\n            bufferTime(bufferWindow),\n            filter(bucket => bucket.length > 0),\n            map(bucket => this.correlateBucket(bucket))\n        );\n\n        // Subscribe once and dispatch to observers.\n        const sub = correlated$.subscribe({\n            next: event => this.dispatch(event),\n            error: err => 'metric'; event: SystemMetricEvent }\n            | { type: 'social'; event: SocialSignalEvent }\n        >\n    ): CorrelatedEvent {\n        const metrics = bucket\n            .filter(b => b.type SocialSignalEvent);\n\n        // Naively pick latest metric and social signal in this window.\n        const latestMetric =\n            metrics.sort((a, b) => b.timestamp - a.timestamp)[0] ??\n            ({\n                timestamp: Date.now(),\n                host: 'unknown',\n                metric: 'unknown',\n                value: 0\n            } as SystemMetricEvent);\n\n        const timestamp: Date.now(),\n            metricHost: latestMetric.host,\n            metricName: latestMetric.metric,\n            metricValue: latestMetric.value,\n            socialSignal: latestSocial,\n            score,\n            riskLevel: 'LOW' // will be overwritten by EnrichmentStep\n        };\n    }\n\n    /* ------------------------------------------------------------------ *\n     *  Internal \u2014 Pipeline dispatch\n     * ------------------------------------------------------------------ */\n\n    private async dispatch(event: CorrelatedEvent): Promise<void> {\n        const invokePipeline = async (index: number): Promise<void> => {\n            if (index >= this.pipeline.length) return;\n            const step = this.pipeline[index];\n            await step.handle(event, () => invokePipeline(index + 1));\n        };\n\n        try {\n            await invokePipeline(0);\n            for (const obs of this.observers) {\n                try {\n                    await obs.onCorrelatedEvent(event);\n                } catch (err) {\n                    this.logger.warn('Observer threw error', { err });\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (err) {\n            this.logger.error('Pipeline processing failed', { err });\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/* ============================================================================\n * If a surge is not detected, the chain stops here.\n */\nclass SurgeDetectionHandler extends Handler {\n    private readonly likeThreshold: number;\n    private readonly shareThreshold: number;\n    private readonly liveViewerThreshold: number;\n\n    constructor(logger: Logger, cfg?: { like?: number; share?: number; live?: number }) {\n        super(logger);\n        this.likeThreshold = cfg?.like ?? 1_000;\n        this.shareThreshold = cfg?.share ?? 500;\n        this.liveViewerThreshold = cfg?.live ?? 10_000;\n    }\n\n    protected async process(event: TelemetryEvent):  Strategy Pattern for scaling algorithms\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport interface ScalingStrategy {\n    /**\n     * Calculates how many replicas are needed to sustain observed load.\n     *\n     * @param currentReplicas Current number of replicas in the cluster\n     * @param event           Event responsible for triggering scaling evaluation\n     */\n    computeDesiredReplicas(currentReplicas: number, event: TelemetryEvent): number;\n}\n\nclass AggressiveScalingStrategy implements ScalingStrategy {\n    computeDesiredReplicas(currentReplicas: number, event: TelemetryEvent): number {\n        // Scale up quickly: +50% replicas per detection\n        return Math.ceil(currentReplicas * 1.5);\n    }\n}\n\nclass ConservativeScalingStrategy implements ScalingStrategy {\n    computeDesiredReplicas(currentReplicas: number, event: TelemetryEvent): number {\n        // Step scaling: +1 replica at a time (bounded)\n        return currentReplicas + 1;\n    }\n}\n\nclass NoopScalingStrategy implements ScalingStrategy {\n    computeDesiredReplicas(currentReplicas: number): number {\n        return currentReplicas; // no scaling\n    }\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// ScalingDecisionHandler extends Handler {\n    private readonly strategy: ScalingStrategy;\n    private readonly clusterIdResolver: (event: TelemetryEvent) => string;\n    private readonly minReplicas: number;\n    private readonly maxReplicas: number;\n\n    constructor(\n        logger: Logger,\n        cfg: {\n            strategy: ScalingStrategy;\n            clusterIdResolver?: (event: TelemetryEvent) => string;\n            minReplicas?: number;\n            maxReplicas?: number;\n        },\n    ) {\n        super(logger);\n        this.strategy = cfg.strategy;\n        this.clusterIdResolver = cfg.clusterIdResolver ?? (() => 'default-cluster');\n        this.minReplicas = cfg.minReplicas ?? 1;\n        this.maxReplicas = cfg.maxReplicas ?? 1_000;\n    }\n\n    protected async process(event: TelemetryEvent, subject: TelemetrySubject): Promise<boolean> {\n        const clusterId = this.clusterIdResolver(event);\n        const currentReplicas = this.resolveCurrentReplicas(clusterId);\n\n        const desired = this.strategy.computeDesiredReplicas(currentReplicas, event);\n        const boundedDesired = Math.max(this.minReplicas, Math.min(this.maxReplicas, desired));\n\n        if (boundedDesired === currentReplicas) {\n            this.logger.info('Scaling evaluation resulted in no changes.', { clusterId });\n            return false; // chain ends\n        }\n\n        const cmd: ScalingCommand = {\n            clusterId,\n            desiredReplicas: boundedDesired,\n            reason: 'social-surge',\n            issuedAt: Date.now(),\n        };\n\n        this.logger.info('Emitting scaling command.', cmd);\n        subject.emit(TelemetrySubject.EVENTS.SCALING_NEEDED, cmd);\n        return false; // end of chain\n    }\n\n    /** Placeholder: in real life we'd query Kubernetes-API, Nomad, etc. */\n    private resolveCurrentReplicas(_clusterId: string): number {\n        return 3; // mock value for demo purposes\n    }\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n//  Public API \u2013 TelemetryProcessor\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport interface TelemetryProcessorOptions {\n    scalingStrategy?: 'aggressive' | 'conservative' | 'noop';\n    validation?: { like?: number; share?: number; live?: number };\n    minReplicas?: number;\n    maxReplicas?: number;\n}\n\n/**\n * Exposes a high-level facade to process telemetry events. Downstream consumers\n * may subscribe to the `subject` property to react to scaling decisions.\n */\nexport class TelemetryProcessor {\n    /** Observer subject for external consumers */\n    public readonly subject = new TelemetrySubject();\n\n    private readonly logger: Logger;\n    private readonly pipeline: Handler;\n\n    constructor(private readonly opts: TelemetryProcessorOptions = {}) {\n        // Create namespaced logger\n        this.logger = createLogger({\n            level: process.env.PS_LOG_LEVEL || 'info',\n            format: format.combine(\n                format.timestamp(),\n                format.errors({ stack: true }),\n                format.splat(),\n                format.json(),\n            ),\n            transports: [new transports.Console()],\n            defaultMeta: { service: 'telemetry-processor' },\n        });\n\n        // Build handler chain\n        const validator = new ValidationHandler(this.logger);\n        const surgeDetector = new SurgeDetectionHandler(this.logger, opts.validation);\n        const scaler = new ScalingDecisionHandler(this.logger, {\n            strategy: TelemetryProcessor.selectStrategy(opts.scalingStrategy),\n            minReplicas: opts.minReplicas,\n            maxReplicas: opts.maxReplicas,\n        });\n\n        validator.setNext(surgeDetector).setNext(scaler);\n        this.pipeline = validator;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Entry-point for new telemetry events.\n     */\n    async ingest(event: TelemetryEvent): Promise<void> {\n        try {\n            await this.pipeline.handle(event, this.subject);\n        } catch (err) {\n            this.logger.error('Unhandled error in telemetry pipeline', { err, event });\n        }\n    }\n\n    //
