Strategy Pattern                                                                              */\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nexport interface AlertStrategy {\n    /**\n     * Evaluate buffered metric & social events, return alerts (if any)\n     * @param metrics  metrics in window\n     * @param signals  social signals in window\n     * @param config   effective config (merged runtime)\n     */\n    evaluate(\n        metrics: ReadonlyArray<MetricEvent>,\n        signals: ReadonlyArray<SocialSignalEvent>,\n        config: AlertingEngineConfig,\n    ): Alert[];\n}\n\n/* ---------- Concrete Strategies ---------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\n/**\n * Trend-based alerting: detects spike in metric vs. baseline, intensifies alert if\n * correlated social amplification observed.\n */\nexport class TrendBasedAlertStrategy implements AlertStrategy {\n    /** Very naive baseline (average of previous window) \u2013 in production use PromQL or similar */\n    private previousAvgMap = new Map<string, number>();\n\n    evaluate(\n        metrics: ReadonlyArray<MetricEvent>,\n        signals: ReadonlyArray<SocialSignalEvent>,\n        config: AlertingEngineConfig,\n    ): Alert[] {\n        const alerts: Alert[] = [];\n\n        const groupedByServiceMetric: Record<string, MetricEvent[]> = {};\n        metrics.forEach((m) => {\n            const key = `${m.service}:${m.metric}`;\n            (groupedByServiceMetric[key] = groupedByServiceMetric[key] || []).push(m);\n        });\n\n        for (const [key, metricEvents] of Object.entries(groupedByServiceMetric)) {\n            const currentAvg =\n                metricEvents.reduce((acc, cur) => acc + cur.value, 0) / metricEvents.length;\n\n            const prevAvg = this.previousAvgMap.get(key) ?? currentAvg;\n            this.previousAvgMap.set(key, currentAvg);\n\n            const deltaRatio = prevAvg === 0 ? 0 : (currentAvg - prevAvg) / prevAvg;\n\n            // simplistic spike detection\n            if (deltaRatio > 0.5) {\n                const [service, metric] = key.split(':');\n                const amplification = signals.reduce((acc, s) => acc + s.weight, 0);\n\n                const severity =\n                    amplification > config.socialAmplificationThreshold\n                        ? AlertSeverity.CRITICAL\n                        : AlertSeverity.WARNING;\n\n                alerts.push({\n                    id: uuid(),\n                    triggeredAt: Date.now(),\n                    service,\n                    metric,\n                    severity,\n                    description: `Trend spike detected (${(\n                        deltaRatio * 100\n                    ).toFixed(1)}%) in ${metric}. Social amplification: ${amplification.toFixed(\n                        2,\n                    )}`,\n                    extraContext: { deltaRatio, amplification, windowSize: metricEvents.length },\n                });\n            }\n        }\n\n        return alerts;\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Sentiment-based strategy: escalate if negative sentiment grows regardless of\n * infrastructure health (meta-monitoring).\n */\nexport class SentimentBasedAlertStrategy implements AlertStrategy {\n    evaluate(\n        metrics: ReadonlyArray<MetricEvent>,\n        signals: ReadonlyArray<SocialSignalEvent>,\n        config: AlertingEngineConfig,\n    ): Alert[] {\n        // Placeholder: suppose weight < 0 is negative sentiment multiplied by magnitude\n        const negativeWeight = signals\n            .filter((s) => s.weight < 0)\n            .reduce((acc, cur) => acc + Math.abs(cur.weight), 0);\n\n        if (negativeWeight === 0) {\n            return [];\n        }\n\n        // escalate in tiers\n        let severity = AlertSeverity.INFO;\n        if (negativeWeight > config.socialAmplificationThreshold * 0.5) {\n            severity = AlertSeverity.WARNING;\n        }\n        if (negativeWeight > config.socialAmplificationThreshold) {\n            severity = AlertSeverity.CRITICAL;\n        }\n\n        // pick an arbitrary metric as context \u2013 not relevant for sentiment\n        const sampleMetric = metrics[0];\n\n        return [\n            {\n                id: uuid(),\n                triggeredAt: Date.now(),\n                service: sampleMetric?.service ?? 'unknown',\n                metric: sampleMetric?.metric ?? 'n/a',\n                severity,\n                description: `Negative sentiment surge detected with aggregate weight ${negativeWeight.toFixed(\n                    2,\n                )}`,\n                extraContext: { negativeWeight },\n            },\n        ];\n    }\n}\n\n/* ---------- Strategy Registry / Factory -------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nexport class StrategyRegistry {\n    private strategies: Map<string, AlertStrategy> = new Map();\n\n    constructor() {\n        // register built-ins\n        this.register('trend', new TrendBasedAlertStrategy());\n        this.register('sentiment', new SentimentBasedAlertStrategy());\n    }\n\n    register(name: string, strategy: AlertStrategy): void {\n        if (this.strategies.has(name)) {\n            throw new Error(`Strategy ${name} already registered`);\n        }\n        this.strategies.set(name, strategy);\n    }\n\n    resolve(name: string): AlertStrategy {\n        const strategy = this.strategies.get(name);\n        if (!strategy) {\n            throw new Error(`Strategy ${name} not found`);\n        }\n        return strategy;\n    }\n}\n\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Social-Aware Alerting Engine (Observer + Strategy)                                            */\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nexport class SocialAwareAlertingService {\n    private subscription?: Subscription;\n    private readonly alertSubject = new Subject<Alert>();\n\n    constructor(\n        private readonly metricStream$: Observable<MetricEvent>,\n        private readonly socialStream$: Observable<SocialSignalEvent>,\n        private readonly configManager: ConfigManager,\n        private readonly strategyRegistry: StrategyRegistry,\n    ) {}\n\n    /**\n     * Start consuming streams & evaluating alerts.\n     */\n    start(): void {\n        if (this.subscription) {\n            throw new Error('Service already started');\n        }\n\n        /* Combine metric & social streams into timed buffers for correlation */\n        const cfg = this.configManager.get();\n        const windowMs = cfg.correlationWindowMs;\n\n        this.subscription = merge(this.metricStream$, this.socialStream$)\n            .pipe(\n                bufferTime(windowMs),\n                filter((buffer) => buffer.length > 0),\n                map((buffer) => {\n                    const metrics: MetricEvent[] = [];\n                    const signals: SocialSignalEvent[] = [];\n                    buffer.forEach((e) => {\n                        if (isMetricEvent(e)) metrics.push(e as MetricEvent);\n                        else signals.push(e as SocialSignalEvent);\n                    });\n                    return { metrics, signals };\n                }),\n                tap(({ metrics, signals }) => {\n                    const effectiveConfig = this.configManager.get();\n                    const strategy = this.strategyRegistry.resolve(effectiveConfig.strategy);\n                    const alerts = strategy.evaluate(metrics, signals, effectiveConfig);\n                    alerts.forEach((alert) => this.alertSubject.next(alert));\n                }),\n            )\n            .subscribe();\n\n        /* Listen for dynamic configuration changes */\n        this.configManager.on('update', (newCfg: AlertingEngineConfig) => {\n            /* Simply log; the next buffer tick will fetch latest config automatically */\n            console.info(\n                `[SocialAwareAlertingService] Config updated: correlationWindowMs=${newCfg.correlationWindowMs}, strategy=${newCfg.strategy}`,\n            );\n        });\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Stop consuming streams gracefully.\n     */\n    stop(): void {\n        this.subscription?.unsubscribe();\n        this.subscription = undefined;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Expose alerts as observable for downstream consumers (PagerDuty, Grafana, etc.)\n     */\n    get alerts$(): Observable<Alert> {\n        return this.alertSubject.asObservable();\n    }\n}\n\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Helper Type Guards                                                                            */\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nfunction isMetricEvent(e: MetricEvent | SocialSignalEvent): e is MetricEvent {\n    return (e as any).metric !== undefined;\n}\n\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n/*  Example Bootstrap (would normally live elsewhere)                                             */\n/* ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- */\n\nif (require.main === module) {\n    // Placeholder sources: In production, these would come from Kafka consumer groups\n    const metricSubject = new Subject<MetricEvent>();\n    const socialSubject = new Subject<SocialSignalEvent>();\n\n    // Create default config\n    const configManager = new ConfigManager({\n        correlationWindowMs: 20_000,\n        socialAmplificationThreshold: 100,\n        strategy: 'trend',\n    });\n\n    // Start the service\n    const service = new SocialAwareAlertingService(\n        metricSubject.asObservable(),\n        socialSubject.asObservable(),\n        configManager,\n        new StrategyRegistry(),\n    );\n\n    service.alerts$.subscribe((alert) => {\n        // send to AlertManager / Slack / etc.\n        console.log(`[ALERT] ${alert.severity} \u2013 ${alert.description}`);\n    });\n\n    service.start();\n\n    /* Mock some events for demonstration */\n    setInterval(() => {\n        metricSubject.next({\n            id: uuid(),\n            timestamp: Date.now(),\n            host: 'node-1',\n            service: 'video-stream',\n            metric: 'cpu_load',\n            value: 30 + Math.random() * 70,\n        });\n    }, 1000);\n\n    setInterval(() => {\n        socialSubject.next({\n            id: uuid(),\n            timestamp: Date.now(),\n            signal: 'live_stream',\n            weight: Math.random() * 20,\n        });\n    }, 800);\n\n    // Simulate hot-reload configuration at runtime\n    setTimeout(() => {\n        configManager.update({ correlationWindowMs: 10_000, strategy: 'sentiment' });\n    }, 60_000);\n}\n```\n",

  "content": "# Solution: typescript_system_monitoring_expert_061_architectural_understanding_expert_01\n\n## Executive Summary\n\nThis architectural analysis traces the end-to-end data flow for a user-defined alerting rule in the PulseSphere SocialOps system monitoring platform. The system employs an **Event-Driven Architecture** with **Publish/Subscribe** patterns as the core decoupling mechanism. The workflow spans 8 primary modules from rule ingestion through notification dispatch.\n\n## Key Files Identified\n\nThe following modules form the critical path for the alerting rule lifecycle:\n\n- `/app/project/src/module_36.ts` - **Configuration Ingestion & Management**: Manages alerting engine configuration with hot-reload capability\n- `/app/project/src/module_42.ts` - **Validation Pipeline**: Contains `ValidationStep` for schema validation using Zod\n- `/app/project/src/module_57.ts` - **Persistence Layer**: Contains `PersistenceStep` for storing correlated events\n- `/app/project/src/module_32.ts` - **Event Bus (Core Infrastructure)**: Defines the `EventBus` class that implements pub/sub communication\n- `/app/project/src/module_4.ts` - **Alert Correlation Engine**: Core engine that buffers telemetry and applies correlation strategies\n- `/app/project/src/module_29.ts` - **Anomaly Detection & Escalation**: Detects anomalies using pluggable strategies and triggers escalation chain\n- `/app/project/src/module_11.ts` - **Notification Dispatch**: Contains PagerDuty, Slack, and Email handlers for alert delivery\n- `/app/project/src/config.ts` - **Configuration Schema**: Defines core data structures and validation schemas\n\nSupporting files:\n- `/app/project/src/constants.ts` - Service names and Kafka topics enumeration\n- `/app/project/src/utils.ts` - Shared utilities including TTLCache for caching\n\n## Code Evidence\n\n### 1. Event Bus Definition (Core Pub/Sub Pattern)\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_32.ts\n// Lines: 182-198\n\n/**\n * Internal EventBus abstraction.  In production we delegate to Kafka or NATS\n * but for local dev / unit testing an EventEmitter is sufficient.\n */\nexport class EventBus extends EventEmitter {\n  publish<T>(topic: string, payload: T) {\n    this.emit(topic, payload);\n  }\n\n  subscribe<T>(\n    topic: string,\n    listener: (payload: T) => void\n  ): () => void /* unsubscribe */ {\n    this.on(topic, listener);\n    return () => this.off(topic, listener);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 2. Configuration Management with Hot-Reload\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_36.ts\n// Lines: 83-102\n\nexport class ConfigManager extends EventEmitter {\n    private current: AlertingEngineConfig;\n\n    constructor(defaults: AlertingEngineConfig) {\n        super();\n        this.current = defaults;\n    }\n\n    get(): AlertingEngineConfig {\n        return { ...this.current };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Hot-reloads current configuration and notifies listeners\n     */\n    update(newConfig: Partial<AlertingEngineConfig>): void {\n        this.current = { ...this.current, ...newConfig };\n        this.emit('update', this.get());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3. Validation Step (Chain-of-Responsibility)\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_42.ts\n// Lines: 211-230\n\nclass ValidationStep extends AbstractStep {\n  async handle({ message, topic, partition }: EachMessagePayload): Promise<void> {\n    try {\n      if (!message.value) throw new Error('Empty message');\n\n      const raw = JSON.parse(message.value.toString());\n      const parsed: RawMetric = RawMetricSchema.parse(raw);\n\n      // Pass parsed object inside message headers for downstream steps\n      message.headers = {\n        ...message.headers,\n        _parsedMetric: Buffer.from(JSON.stringify(parsed)),\n      };\n      await this.nextHandle({ message, topic, partition });\n    } catch (err) {\n      logger.error({ err }, 'Validation failure \u2013 routing to DLQ');\n      await DLQPublisher.publish(message);\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 4. Persistence Step\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_57.ts\n// Lines: 161-174\n\nclass PersistenceStep implements PipelineStep {\n    constructor(private readonly logger: winston.Logger) {}\n\n    async handle(event: CorrelatedEvent, next: () => Promise<void>): Promise<void> {\n        // In production we'd persist into ClickHouse / TimescaleDB or send to Kafka topic.\n        try {\n            this.logger.info('Persisting correlated event', { event });\n        } catch (err) {\n            this.logger.warn('Failed to persist correlated event', { err, event });\n        }\n        await next();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 5. Alert Correlation Engine (Metric Evaluation)\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_4.ts\n// Lines: 241-269\n\nexport class AlertCorrelationEngine {\n  private readonly telemetry$ = new Subject<TelemetryEvent>();\n  private currentStrategy: AlertCorrelationStrategy;\n\n  constructor(private readonly options: EngineOptions) {\n    // Bootstrap initial strategy\n    const initialDescriptor = options.configService.get<StrategyDescriptor>(\n      this.strategyConfigPath\n    );\n    this.currentStrategy = StrategyFactory.create(initialDescriptor);\n\n    // Subscribe to config changes to hot-swap strategies\n    options.configService\n      .onChange(this.strategyConfigPath)\n      .subscribe((newDescriptor) => this.updateStrategy(newDescriptor as StrategyDescriptor));\n\n    // Wire telemetry stream\n    options.telemetryStream$.subscribe({\n      next: (ev) => this.telemetry$.next(ev),\n      error: (err) => this.logger('Telemetry stream failure', err),\n    });\n\n    // Start pipeline\n    this.initProcessingPipeline();\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 6. Notification Dispatch Chain (Chain-of-Responsibility)\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_11.ts\n// Lines: 126-145, 150-180, 185-205\n\nabstract class EscalationHandler {\n  private nextHandler?: EscalationHandler;\n\n  setNext(handler: EscalationHandler): EscalationHandler {\n    this.nextHandler = handler;\n    return handler;\n  }\n\n  async handle(alert: Alert): Promise<void> {\n    const processed = await this.process(alert);\n    if (!processed && this.nextHandler) {\n      await this.nextHandler.handle(alert);\n    }\n  }\n\n  protected abstract process(alert: Alert): Promise<boolean>;\n}\n\nclass PagerDutyHandler extends EscalationHandler { /* ... */ }\nclass SlackHandler extends EscalationHandler { /* ... */ }\nclass EmailHandler extends EscalationHandler { /* ... */ }\n```\n\n### 7. Bootstrap Wiring - Notification Chain Assembly\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_11.ts\n// Lines: 381-385\n\n// Build escalation chain: PagerDuty \u2192 Slack \u2192 Email\nconst pagerDuty = new PagerDutyHandler(process.env.PAGERDUTY_KEY ?? 'dummy');\nconst slack = new SlackHandler(process.env.SLACK_WEBHOOK ?? 'https://hooks.slack.com/services/dummy');\nconst email = new EmailHandler(process.env.SMTP_ENDPOINT ?? 'https://smtp.internal');\npagerDuty.setNext(slack).setNext(email);\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Core Architectural Pattern: Event-Driven / Publish-Subscribe\n\nThe PulseSphere SocialOps platform uses an **Event-Driven Architecture** with **Publish/Subscribe** (pub/sub) as the primary decoupling mechanism. This is evidenced by:\n\n1. **EventBus Class** (`module_32.ts`): A central abstraction that wraps Node.js EventEmitter, providing `publish()` and `subscribe()` methods for topic-based communication.\n\n2. **Kafka/NATS Integration**: Multiple modules consume from Kafka topics and publish to NATS subjects, demonstrating distributed messaging patterns.\n\n3. **RxJS Observables**: Used extensively for reactive stream processing and event correlation.\n\n### Data Flow Sequence for Alerting Rule Lifecycle\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502                    ALERTING RULE DATA FLOW SEQUENCE                         \u2502\n\u251c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2524\n\u2502                                                                             \u2502\n\u2502  1. Event Bus Definition (Core Pub/Sub Pattern)\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_32.ts\n// Lines: 182-198\n\n/**\n * Internal EventBus abstraction.  In production we delegate to Kafka or NATS\n * but for local dev / unit testing an EventEmitter is sufficient.\n */\nexport class EventBus extends EventEmitter {\n  publish<T>(topic: string, payload: T) {\n    this.emit(topic, payload);\n  }\n\n  subscribe<T>(\n    topic: string,\n    listener: (payload: T) => void\n  ): () => void /* unsubscribe */ {\n    this.on(topic, listener);\n    return () => this.off(topic, listener);\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 2. Configuration Management with Hot-Reload\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_36.ts\n// Lines: 83-102\n\nexport class ConfigManager extends EventEmitter {\n    private current: AlertingEngineConfig;\n\n    constructor(defaults: AlertingEngineConfig) {\n        super();\n        this.current = defaults;\n    }\n\n    get(): AlertingEngineConfig {\n        return { ...this.current };\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Hot-reloads current configuration and notifies listeners\n     */\n    update(newConfig: Partial<AlertingEngineConfig>): void {\n        this.current = { ...this.current, ...newConfig };\n        this.emit('update', this.get());\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3. Validation Step (Chain-of-Responsibility)\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_42.ts\n// Lines: 211-230\n\nclass ValidationStep extends AbstractStep {\n  async handle({ message, topic, partition }: EachMessagePayload): Promise<void> {\n    try {\n      if (!message.value) throw new Error('Empty message');\n\n      const raw = JSON.parse(message.value.toString());\n      const parsed: RawMetric = RawMetricSchema.parse(raw);\n\n      // Pass parsed object inside message headers for downstream steps\n      message.headers = {\n        ...message.headers,\n        _parsedMetric: Buffer.from(JSON.stringify(parsed)),\n      };\n      await this.nextHandle({ message, topic, partition });\n    } catch (err) {\n      logger.error({ err }, 'Validation failure \u2013 routing to DLQ');\n      await DLQPublisher.publish(message);\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 4. Persistence Step\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_57.ts\n// Lines: 161-174\n\nclass PersistenceStep implements PipelineStep {\n    constructor(private readonly logger: winston.Logger) {}\n\n    async handle(event: CorrelatedEvent, next: () => Promise<void>): Promise<void> {\n        // In production we'd persist into ClickHouse / TimescaleDB or send to Kafka topic.\n        try {\n            this.logger.info('Persisting correlated event', { event });\n        } catch (err) {\n            this.logger.warn('Failed to persist correlated event', { err, event });\n        }\n        await next();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 5. Alert Correlation Engine (Metric Evaluation)\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_4.ts\n// Lines: 241-269\n\nexport class AlertCorrelationEngine {\n  private readonly telemetry$ = new Subject<TelemetryEvent>();\n  private currentStrategy: AlertCorrelationStrategy;\n\n  constructor(private readonly options: EngineOptions) {\n    // Bootstrap initial strategy\n    const initialDescriptor = options.configService.get<StrategyDescriptor>(\n      this.strategyConfigPath\n    );\n    this.currentStrategy = StrategyFactory.create(initialDescriptor);\n\n    // Subscribe to config changes to hot-swap strategies\n    options.configService\n      .onChange(this.strategyConfigPath)\n      .subscribe((newDescriptor) => this.updateStrategy(newDescriptor as StrategyDescriptor));\n\n    // Wire telemetry stream\n    options.telemetryStream$.subscribe({\n      next: (ev) => this.telemetry$.next(ev),\n      error: (err) => this.logger('Telemetry stream failure', err),\n    });\n\n    // Start pipeline\n    this.initProcessingPipeline();\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 6. Notification Dispatch Chain (Chain-of-Responsibility)\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_11.ts\n// Lines: 126-145, 150-180, 185-205\n\nabstract class EscalationHandler {\n  private nextHandler?: EscalationHandler;\n\n  setNext(handler: EscalationHandler): EscalationHandler {\n    this.nextHandler = handler;\n    return handler;\n  }\n\n  async handle(alert: Alert): Promise<void> {\n    const processed = await this.process(alert);\n    if (!processed && this.nextHandler) {\n      await this.nextHandler.handle(alert);\n    }\n  }\n\n  protected abstract process(alert: Alert): Promise<boolean>;\n}\n\nclass PagerDutyHandler extends EscalationHandler { /* ... */ }\nclass SlackHandler extends EscalationHandler { /* ... */ }\nclass EmailHandler extends EscalationHandler { /* ... */ }\n```\n\n### 7. Bootstrap Wiring - Notification Chain Assembly\n```typescript\n// File: /app/project/src/module_11.ts\n// Lines: 381-385\n\n// Build escalation chain: PagerDuty \u2192 Slack \u2192 Email\nconst pagerDuty = new PagerDutyHandler(process.env.PAGERDUTY_KEY ?? 'dummy');\nconst slack = new SlackHandler(process.env.SLACK_WEBHOOK ?? 'https://hooks.slack.com/services/dummy');\nconst email = new EmailHandler(process.env.SMTP_ENDPOINT ?? 'https://smtp.internal');\npagerDuty.setNext(slack).setNext(email);\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Core Architectural Pattern: Event-Driven / Publish-Subscribe\n\nThe PulseSphere SocialOps platform uses an **Event-Driven Architecture** with **Publish/Subscribe** (pub/sub) as the primary decoupling mechanism. # Solution: typescript_system_monitoring_expert_061_architectural_understanding_expert_01

## Executive Summary

This architectural analysis traces the end-to-end data flow for a user-defined alerting rule in the PulseSphere SocialOps system monitoring platform. The system employs an **Event-Driven Architecture** with **Publish/Subscribe** patterns as the core decoupling mechanism. The workflow spans 8 primary modules from rule ingestion through notification dispatch.

## Key Files Identified

The following modules form the critical path for the alerting rule lifecycle:

- `/app/project/src/module_36.ts` - **Configuration Ingestion & Management**: Manages alerting engine configuration with hot-reload capability
- `/app/project/src/module_42.ts` - **Validation Pipeline**: Contains `ValidationStep` for schema validation using Zod
- `/app/project/src/module_57.ts` - **Persistence Layer**: Contains `PersistenceStep` for storing correlated events
- `/app/project/src/module_32.ts` - **Event Bus (Core Infrastructure)**: Defines the `EventBus` class that implements pub/sub communication
- `/app/project/src/module_4.ts` - **Alert Correlation Engine**: Core engine that buffers telemetry and applies correlation strategies
- `/app/project/src/module_29.ts` - **Anomaly Detection & Escalation**: Detects anomalies using pluggable strategies and triggers escalation chain
- `/app/project/src/module_11.ts` - **Notification Dispatch**: Contains PagerDuty, Slack, and Email handlers for alert delivery
- `/app/project/src/config.ts` - **Configuration Schema**: Defines core data structures and validation schemas

Supporting files:
- `/app/project/src/constants.ts` - Service names and Kafka topics enumeration
- `/app/project/src/utils.ts` - Shared utilities including TTLCache for caching
